PHASE 2 (P1 — the real upgrade): surface the rich NormalizedPR signal in PR rows (reviewDecision pill, checksStatus k/n, comment count) and add the Review subview to the PR detail by reusing the existing PRHeader/ChecksSection/CommentsSection primitives over a NormalizedPR fetched for the previewed PR; add the segmented Открытые/На ревью/Влитые/Закрытые filter (needs the backend to return reviewDecision/checks — extend the host searchPullRequests json fields to include reviewDecision/statusCheckRollup, which gh pr list already supports). Add framer-motion list/pill motion with prefers-reduced-motion guards.

PHASE 3 (P2 — power-user + linkage): ⌘K command palette (cmdk or @rox/ui Command), j/k/Enter keyboard nav, task↔PR↔issue cross-chips backed by a local @tanstack/react-db linkage collection, optional promotion of the PR list to a sortable TanStack Table column model, and relative timestamps via date-fns ru locale. Defer anything requiring new cloud endpoints.

### Settings (app / provider / account) — desktop surface at route /_authenticated/settings/* (TanStack file route, NOT a _dashboard child). Shell: apps/desktop/src/renderer/routes/_authenticated/settings/layout.tsx. 17 leaf sections grouped into 4 nav groups (Личное / Редактор и процесс / Организация / Система) plus three inner-sidebar sections (projects, hosts, agents). Search registry + zustand state: apps/desktop/src/renderer/stores/settings-state.ts and .../settings/utils/settings-search/settings-search.ts. Three data planes already wired: electronTrpc (local app prefs), chatServiceTrpc (provider OAuth/keys via IPC), apiTrpcClient/cloudTrpc + @tanstack/react-db useLiveQuery (account/org/Electric). — приоритет `P0`
**Назначение:** Single hub where a solo-founder configures (a) the app itself — appearance/glass/fonts/motion/notifications/keyboard/behavior/git/terminal/links, (b) AI providers — ROX R1, Anthropic/OpenAI OAuth or API key, Groq/Google/DeepSeek keys, custom OpenAI-compatible endpoints, plus per-provider env overrides, and (c) the account & org — profile, identity links, usage/balance, members, teams, API keys, integrations, hosts, permissions, security, experiments. It is the control plane that makes every other surface (Chat, Pipelines, Notes, Mail) behave correctly and look right. Grounding: this is already ~90% built; the work is an upgrade — collapse the triple-maintained registry into one source of truth, add a shared glass SettingsCard primitive, deep-link from the command palette into a specific setting row, and add dirty/reset affordances — not a greenfield rebuild.

**UX:** LAYOUT (keep current shell, harden it). Full-screen flex column on bg-tertiary. Top: 48px (h-12) draggable titlebar, paddingLeft 96px on macOS (traffic-light inset) else 8px, hosting NavigationControls (back/forward). Body: flex row — left 224px (w-56) SettingsSidebar, right content pane in m-3 bg-background rounded overflow-auto. Sidebar: "Назад" back-link to originRoute, "Настройки" H1, search input (bg-accent/50, magnifier left, clear-X right), 4 nav groups with [10px] uppercase tracking-[0.1em] muted labels, rows px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md, active row uses framer-motion layoutId="settings-nav-active" pill (motionSpring.snappy) + text-accent-foreground, hover bg-accent/50, trailing per-section match-count badge during search; footer 3 docs links (Навыки/MCP/Документация). Content pane: AnimatePresence mode="wait" initial={false}, section keyed opacity crossfade (motionDuration.fast, ease.standard), wrapped mx-auto w-full max-w-7xl except the three inner-sidebar sections (projects/hosts/agents) which render their own SettingsListSidebar (w-64, border-r). Each leaf page: p-6 max-w-4xl/5xl, header H2 text-xl font-semibold + text-sm muted subtitle (mb-8), then space-y-6/8 list of sections; every section owns its own data fetching so one query resolving never re-renders siblings.

DARK GLASS / VICTOR MONO / RU. Inherits global .glass document-root class + window-opacity CSS vars (driven by electronTrpc.window.setGlass, optimistic with rollback). NEW shared primitive SettingsCard: rounded-lg border border-border/60, bg-card/60 supports-[backdrop-filter]:bg-card/40 backdrop-blur-xl when .glass is on (falls back to solid bg-card when glass off or non-mac), inner divide-y divide-border/60 for stacked rows. Replaces the three ad-hoc card shapes today (GlassSection's rounded-lg border divide-y, ModelsSettings SettingsSection, AccountSettings inline SettingRow). Headings/body use the app font stack; all monospace values (model IDs, Base URLs, API-key env names, branch prefixes, paths, keyboard accelerators) render in font-mono (Victor Mono). All copy in Russian (existing: "Внешний вид", "Остекление", "Непрозрачность окна", "Модели", "Аккаунт", "Выйти", "Подключить заново"); EN allowed only for proper nouns (Anthropic, OpenAI, GitHub, MCP) and code tokens.

COMPONENTS (shadcn/Radix already in use): Switch (toggles: glass, confirm-quit, resource-monitor, security relay, experimental flags), Slider (window opacity, font size), Input type=password (API keys, font-mono), Collapsible (Anthropic "Дополнительно" advanced env), Select/RadioGroup (theme, markdown style, file-open mode, animation tier, font family), Dialog/AlertDialog (generate API key, delete key, sign-out confirm, slug change), Badge (provider status: Не подключено/Истекло/Требует внимания/Активно), Avatar (profile), Skeleton + ProfileSkeleton (loading), Sonner toast (every save), Tooltip (permission help, mac-only hints), Command (cmdk) for the NEW deep-link palette.

INTERACTIONS. Provider auth: OAuth via AnthropicOAuthDialog/OpenAIOAuthDialog launched by useAnthropicOAuth/useOpenAIOAuth, status Badge + contextual action button (Войти / Подключить заново / Выйти). API keys: Input + Save/Clear (ConfigRow), masked, save on explicit button, env-config advanced fields save on blur. Account name: blur-to-save (handleNameBlur) with rollback + toast; avatar via electronTrpc.window.selectImageFile -> apiTrpcClient.user.uploadAvatar. App prefs: optimistic electronTrpc writes (onMutate sets data + applies CSS immediately, onError rolls back). Search: typing in sidebar filters the whole registry; sections with zero matches hide from nav; if active section has no matches, layout auto-navigates (replace) to first matching section; SearchResultsBanner shows count + clear. Escape pops one route segment (or back to originRoute at depth<=2). NEW: command palette action "Открыть настройку: <title>" navigates to /settings/<section> with a #anchor + briefly highlights the target SettingsCard (RevealFlash/HighlightFlash from @rox/ui/motion). NEW: per-section "Сбросить к значениям по умолчанию" affordance where a default exists (glass opacity, fonts, animation tier).

MOTION. Use @rox/ui/motion tokens only (no one-off CSS): section crossfade motionDuration.fast; nav active pill motionSpring.snappy via shared layoutId; match-count badge pop motionSpring.badge; advanced-config Collapsible height via AnimatedHeight; save success uses existing toast (MotionToast); form save failure shake via shakeVariants/motionShake (motion controls). All gated by useShouldAnimate("decorative"|"essential") so the Анимации=выключено tier (already a setting) disables them. Respect prefers-reduced-motion through useMotionPreference.

EMPTY / LOADING / ERROR. Loading: ProfileSkeleton (account), @rox/ui/skeleton rows (integrations, api-keys, members, hosts). Cache-first rule (AGENTS.md #9): never blank an existing row because a live collection is not yet ready — fall back to authClient.useSession user. Empty: API keys -> "Создать API-ключ" CTA card; integrations -> per-provider Подключить buttons; teams/members -> friendly text. Error: provider status Badge "Требует внимания"/"Истекло" + reconnect; mutation failure -> toast.error with server message; mac-only sections (Разрешения) hidden off-macOS; v1-only/v2-only items hidden by SETTING_ITEM_VARIANT so counts and visibility agree. Offline/host-down: local electronTrpc prefs still editable; cloud-backed sections (account/org/api-keys) show inline "нет связи" without destroying cached values.

**Функционал:**
- Navigate a 17-section, 4-group settings hub with a sticky 224px sidebar, animated active indicator, and full-text RU+EN search across ~90 registered settings with per-section match counts (settings-search registry).
- Appearance: switch theme, import custom themes, toggle Остекление (glass) + adjust window opacity slider with live native vibrancy, pick wallpaper with auto-rotate, toggle loading-screen quote, choose markdown style, set animation tier (Анимации), and configure editor + terminal fonts (family/size, incl. Victor Mono) — all via optimistic electronTrpc writes that apply CSS immediately and roll back on error.
- Providers (Модели): use free ROX R1 by default; connect Anthropic and OpenAI via OAuth dialogs or API key; add Groq / Google Gemini / DeepSeek API keys; configure a custom OpenAI-compatible provider (Base URL + key); set Anthropic advanced env overrides (auth token, base URL, extra env) saved on blur; see live status badges (Не подключено/Истекло/Требует внимания/Активно) and disconnect.
- Account: edit display name (blur-to-save), upload avatar, view read-only email, manage identity (linked GitHub/Telegram/username) and public profile, view balance/usage/sessions ledger (AccountUsagePanel), and sign out of this device with confirmation.
- Organization & teams: rename org, edit slug (dialog), copy org ID, manage members + roles, send/cancel invites, view pending invitations, and create/rename/delete teams.
- API keys: list, generate (dialog -> one-time reveal + copy), and revoke API keys for external MCP access, backed by Electric useLiveQuery so the list updates live.
- Integrations: connect/disconnect Linear, GitHub (installation), Slack, Telegram, Discord, Notion, Obsidian, Fibery, Lark from a single grid with provider icons and status.
- Hosts: per-host members/roles, invite to host, set default worktree location (inner SettingsListSidebar of hosts).
- System: toggle macOS permissions (Full Disk / Accessibility / Microphone / Apple Events / Local Network, mac-only), toggle the security relay exposure, and flip experimental feature flags (Agent-Native Team OS, v1->v2 migration, rerun onboarding).
- Behavior/Git/Terminal/Links/Keyboard: confirm-on-quit, resource monitor, file-open mode, branch prefix + worktree location, terminal presets/quick-add/sessions, file vs URL vs sidebar link-open behavior, and keyboard shortcuts incl. push-to-talk accelerator.
- Deep-link: from the command palette (cmdk) jump straight to any setting row, which navigates to the owning section and briefly highlights the target card.
- Search-aware routing: empty-match sections vanish from the sidebar and the app auto-redirects to the first section that has matches; clearing search restores full nav.

**OSS-источники:**
- **shadcn/ui** (`github.com/shadcn-ui/ui (components vendored in packages/ui)`, MIT) — заимствуем: Settings-page composition recipes and the Tabs/Card/Form/Switch/Slider/Select/Dialog/Collapsible building blocks; specifically the 'settings form section' layout (label+description left, control right) to formalize the shared SettingsCard + SettingsRow primitive that today is copy-pasted three ways (GlassSection, ModelsSettings SettingsSection, AccountSettings inline SettingRow). · стек-фит: Already the foundation — Radix primitives + Tailwind v4, React 19, copy-in (not a runtime dep). Zero new dependency; pure pattern consolidation.
- **Radix UI Primitives** (`@radix-ui/react-* (react-dialog 1.1.15, react-label 2.1.8 already in apps/desktop)`, MIT) — заимствуем: Accessible Switch, Slider, Tabs, RadioGroup, Collapsible, Tooltip, ScrollArea, Toggle-Group primitives for the new/normalized controls (animation tier, theme, file-open mode) so keyboard + a11y come for free; ScrollArea for long sidebar/section overflow. · стек-фит: Headless, already the design-system base. Add only the @radix-ui packages not yet installed (radio-group, toggle-group, scroll-area, tooltip).
- **cmdk** (`github.com/pacocoursey/cmdk (npm: cmdk)`, MIT) — заимствуем: Command-menu list/keyboard-nav engine to power the NEW 'open a specific setting' deep-link palette, sourced directly from the existing SETTINGS_ITEMS registry (title + RU/EN keywords already present) — the registry becomes both the search index and the palette index. · стек-фит: React + headless, used by shadcn's Command; repo already has a commandPalette/modules/settings module to extend. Tiny, MIT, Tailwind-styleable.
- **TanStack Virtual** (`github.com/TanStack/virtual (npm: @tanstack/react-virtual)`, MIT) — заимствуем: Row virtualization for long lists that currently render fully — org members, host members, keyboard-shortcut table, and integration grids — to keep the glass/backdrop-blur panes at 60fps on large orgs. · стек-фит: Same TanStack family already in use (router/query/db 0.1.83). Headless, React 19 compatible, no styling opinions.
- **React Hook Form + @hookform/resolvers + Zod** (`react-hook-form (7.72.0), @hookform/resolvers (5.2.2), zod (4.3.6) — all already installed`, MIT) — заимствуем: Adopt the SlugDialog RHF+zod pattern (already in-repo) as the standard for multi-field provider/org forms (custom provider Base URL+key+headers, Anthropic advanced env, invite-member) to replace fragile ad-hoc blur-save useState chains and get inline validation + dirty-tracking (enables the Сбросить/reset affordance). · стек-фит: Already in apps/desktop; tRPC inputs are zod schemas so the same schema validates client + server. No new dependency.
- **sonner** (`github.com/emilkowalski/sonner (re-exported as @rox/ui/sonner)`, MIT) — заимствуем: Keep as the single save-feedback channel (toast.success/toast.error) already used by every settings mutation; standardize success/err copy in the shared SettingsCard save helper. · стек-фит: Already wired via @rox/ui/sonner; React 19 + framer-motion friendly.
- **framer-motion (motion)** (`github.com/motiondivision/motion (npm: framer-motion 12.38.0, exposed via @rox/ui/motion)`, MIT) — заимствуем: Reuse the existing motion token kit (motionDuration/motionSpring/ease, layoutId shared-element pill, AnimatedHeight, HighlightFlash/RevealFlash, shakeVariants) for the section crossfade, nav pill, collapsible advanced config, deep-link target highlight, and save-error shake — no new motion code, just call existing primitives. · стек-фит: Already the app's motion layer with a documented append-only token file; gated by useShouldAnimate so the Анимации setting controls it.

**npm:** `cmdk@^1.0.0`, `@tanstack/react-virtual@^3.10.0`, `@radix-ui/react-scroll-area@^1.2.0`, `@radix-ui/react-tooltip@^1.1.0`, `@radix-ui/react-radio-group@^1.2.0`, `@radix-ui/react-toggle-group@^1.1.0`

**Фазинг:** MVP (P0, ships first — hardening of what already works): 1) Extract a single source-of-truth settings manifest that drives the route map (layout.tsx), the nav groups (GeneralSettings), and the search registry (settings-search) — today these three are maintained by hand and drift; collapse to one typed array (id/section/route/label/icon/variant/keywords). 2) Introduce shared SettingsCard + SettingsRow glass primitive (bg-card/40 backdrop-blur-xl under .glass, solid fallback) and migrate GlassSection, ModelsSettings.SettingsSection, AccountSettings.SettingRow onto it so every section is visually consistent and Victor-Mono mono-values are uniform. 3) Verify the Модели provider flow end-to-end (OAuth dialogs, key save/clear, status badges) and the optimistic electronTrpc appearance writes with rollback. 4) Keep RU localization complete across all 17 sections. Acceptance: dark-glass screenshot via Peekaboo of Appearance + Модели + Аккаунт matching intent (RU, Victor Mono, glass), zero TS/lint errors, search counts agree with visible sections.\n\nP1 (next): 5) Command-palette deep-link into a specific setting row (cmdk over the unified manifest) with HighlightFlash on arrival, extending commandPalette/modules/settings. 6) Dirty-state + 'Сбросить к значениям по умолчанию' per setting where a default exists (glass opacity, fonts, animation tier), built on RHF dirty tracking. 7) Adopt the SlugDialog RHF+zod pattern for custom-provider and invite-member forms (replace ad-hoc blur-save useState). 8) Tooltips on mac-only/permission rows.\n\nP2 (later): 9) Virtualize long lists (org members, host members, keyboard shortcut table, integrations) with @tanstack/react-virtual for 60fps under large orgs. 10) Settings sync/export-import of app-pref subset. 11) Mobile/web parity adapters — the unified manifest + headless controls already make the slices reusable; apps/mobile and apps/web settings screens consume the same manifest with platform-specific shells (multiplatform-first).

---

## 3. Карта поверхностей (recon)

### Pipelines (agent graph editor)
- **Entry:** Index: /_authenticated/_dashboard/pipelines/ (page.tsx -> PipelinesIndex). Editor: /_authenticated/_dashboard/pipelines/$pipelineId/ (page.tsx -> PipelineEditor). Data is CLOUD (Neon) via cloudTrpc.pipeline.*, NOT Electric.
- **Состояние:** Fully implemented and functional. Index lists org pipelines (cloudTrpc.pipeline.list) as cards + create-from-template dialog or empty-state gallery; createDraft seeds chosen template graph and navigates to editor. Editor (PipelineEditor.tsx) holds the authoritative RoxWorkflowState in useState seeded from initialPipeline.draftState; renders an @xyflow/react canvas (PipelineCanvas) with 5 node kinds (start, agent_run, human_approval=Подтверждение, loop=Цикл, response=Финал) plus a right panel that is either the NodeInspector (when a node is selected) or 3 tabs (Роли / Триггеры / Запуски). Graph edits debounce-save (800ms) via pipeline.updateGraph; a SaveIndicator shows saving/saved. Toolbar shows a validity Badge (граф валиден | N проблем(ы)).
- **Gaps:** NODE ADD: two paths, both -> addNode() in PipelineEditor.tsx (line 186). (1) Canvas top-left Panel has 4 ghost buttons (Агент/Цикл/Подтверждение/Финал) calling onAddNode(kind). (2) RoleLibraryPanel rows call addRoleNode(slug,label) -> addNode('agent_run', roleSlug, label). addNode generates id `${kind}_${rand}`, lays out in a cascade (180+(count%4)*280 x), writes subBlocks.roleSlug, then selects the node to open the inspector. Edges are added via xyflow onConnect (PipelineCanvas handleConnect). NOTE: newly added nodes are NOT auto-connected to anything, so they are immediately 'unreachable from start' until the user draws an edge.
VALIDATION / PROBLEMS: come from validateGraph() in @rox/workflow-core (validateGraph.ts) via cloudTrpc.pipeline.validate. validateGraph checks: exactly one start block, every edge references existing nodes, no cycles, reachability from start (UNREACHABLE_BLOCK / DISABLED_BRIDGE_BLOCK), unknown block types only when strictBlockTypes (NOT set here), and skill-input mappings only when resolveSkillInputSchema is provided (NOT provided here). KEY SUBTLETY: the editor builds validateInput = useMemo(() => ({ pipelineId }), [pipelineId]) (PipelineEditor.tsx line 81) and never passes draftState, even though validatePipelineSchema supports draftState (schema.ts line 69). So pipeline.validate ALWAYS reads the PERSISTED DB draftState, not the live in-memory graph. validation refreshes only after a successful updateGraph mutation invalidates the validate queryKey (lines 103-105). Net effect: the 'N проблем' badge and per-node issue list lag the live canvas by the 800ms debounce + round-trip; right after adding a node the badge is stale until the save lands.
NODE CONFIG 'DISABLED' PREMISE: In the CURRENT code the agent config is NOT disabled. AgentNodeForm.tsx renders an enabled Role Select, plus enabled Model-override / Макс. шагов (maxTurns) / Температура (temperature) inputs that commit via patch.patchNode -> subBlocksPatch/deleteSubBlockKeys. There are NO `disabled` attributes on these inputs (grep confirms the only `disabled` usages in the editor are seed/create/run buttons). The only gating is advisory TEXT: 'Узел не выполнится без привязанной роли' when no roleSlug, and 'Роль не найдена: <slug>' when the bound slug is not in agentRole.list. The Start node has NO editable body by design (StartNodeForm is just helper text; rename is in the inspector header; delete is hidden for start via isStart). If a deployed build appears to show disabled agent config, it does not match this source — likely a stale build, a different/older bundle, or the roles list failing to load (agentRole.list error) leaving the Select with only 'Без роли'. Worth verifying which build is running.

### Automations
- **Entry:** List: /_authenticated/_dashboard/automations/ (page.tsx -> AutomationsPage). Detail: /_authenticated/_dashboard/automations/$automationId (page.tsx). layout.tsx is a bare <Outlet/>. List data is ELECTRIC live-query (collections.automations); mutations go through apiTrpcClient.automation.* (cloud).
- **Состояние:** Fully implemented. List page is a dense grid table with Мои/Команда scope tabs (counts), columns Название/Проект/Рабочее пространство/Устройство/Агент/Расписание + a per-row kebab menu (Редактировать / Запустить сейчас / История версий / Удалить). Rows resolve project/user/workspace/host via separate Electric live-queries into Maps; schedule rendered via describeSchedule(rrule) from @rox/shared/rrule. Enabled state shown as a colored dot + 'на паузе' badge. Empty states differ per scope (mine -> AutomationsEmptyState template gallery; team -> Empty illustration). Delete uses an AlertDialog; runNow/delete fire toasts. Detail page (AutomationBody) edits name (EmojiTextInput) + prompt (MarkdownEditor with project file search) and autosaves via automation.update / automation.setPrompt; has version history sheet + previous-runs list + a properties sidebar.
- **Gaps:** No obvious placeholders. Robust against Electric sync churn (filters nullish rows from live queries, referencing issue #4519). Real risk areas: heavy fan-out of live-queries (users, projects, workspaces, hosts) on the list; 'Удалено'/'Авто' fallbacks when a referenced workspace/host is missing. Depends on cloud apiTrpcClient for all writes, so offline/host-down degrades actions (not the list).

### Tasks and PR
- **Entry:** Tasks index: /_authenticated/_dashboard/tasks/ (page.tsx -> TasksView). PR preview: /_authenticated/_dashboard/tasks/pr/$prNumber. Issue preview: /_authenticated/_dashboard/tasks/issue/$issueNumber. Task detail: /_authenticated/_dashboard/tasks/$taskId. Type sub-tabs (tasks|prs|issues), view (table|board), and filters are URL-search driven (tasks/layout.tsx + stores/tasks-filter-state.ts).
- **Состояние:** Fully implemented. TasksView is a controlled shell: TasksTopBar (tabs all/active/backlog, search w/ 300ms URL debounce, assignee + project filters, view toggle, type tabs) over one of three content panes. tasks pane = TableContent or BoardContent (kanban) over Electric task collections (useTasksData). prs pane = PullRequestsContent: infinite-scroll list (useInfiniteQuery, PAGE_SIZE 30, IntersectionObserver) fetched from the HOST service client (getHostServiceClientByUrl(hostUrl).workspaceCreation.searchPullRequests), not cloud tRPC; rows show PRIcon/state, #num, title, author, open-in-browser + 'В рабочее пространство' (opens new-workspace modal with linkedPR). issues pane = GitHubIssuesContent. When Linear is not connected and type=tasks, the whole pane is replaced by LinearCTA. Auto-selects the first v2 project into the URL if none chosen.
- **Gaps:** PR/issue panes hard-depend on a reachable host (hostUrl) and a selected project — both gate to friendly empty/placeholder text ('Выберите проект, чтобы увидеть PR', 'Нет открытых PR', repoMismatch hint) rather than real failure surfacing; retry:false so transient host errors just show error text. Tasks pane depends on Linear/Electric; without Linear the tasks tab is entirely CTA. No client cycle/state issues observed.

### Workspaces sidebar
- **Entry:** Two distinct things: (A) Workspaces LIST route /_authenticated/_dashboard/workspaces/ (page.tsx -> WorkspacesListView, a full-screen grouped list, host/electron tRPC). (B) The in-workspace SIDEBAR: WorkspaceSidebar under /_authenticated/_dashboard/v2-workspace/$workspaceId/components/WorkspaceSidebar (Files/Changes/Review tabs + PR action header), rendered inside a v2 workspace.
- **Состояние:** Both fully implemented. (A) WorkspacesListView: filter toggle (Все/Активные/Закрытые with counts) + search; merges OPEN workspaces (workspaces.getAllGrouped) and CLOSED worktrees (workspaces.getWorktreesByProject per recent project) into one list grouped by project, sorted active-first then by lastOpenedAt; rows animate in (MotionList); switch navigates, reopen calls workspaces.openWorktree; includes gated ProjectObjectGraphSection ('Project OS'). (B) WorkspaceSidebar: a PRActionHeader on top + a SidebarHeader tab bar (Файлы/Changes/Review) whose active tab persists in Electric v2WorkspaceLocalState.sidebarState.activeTab. Uses a ResizeObserver with hysteresis (compact when width<260, expand when >280) to collapse tab labels. FilesTab = file tree with git status, Changes tab = diff/commit range UI, Review tab = PR comments.
- **Gaps:** PRActionHeader 'Create PR' is gated by a hardcoded const CREATE_PR_BUTTON_ENABLED = true (WorkspaceSidebar.tsx line 26) — a feature flag left ON in source; genuinely-invalid states (no repo / default branch / detached HEAD) still disable via selectActionButton. The chat-driven create flow dispatches '/pr/create-pr' into a chat pane via onOpenChat. Sidebar tab switching no-ops if v2WorkspaceLocalState row for the workspace is absent (guards `if (!collections.v2WorkspaceLocalState.get(workspaceId)) return`). List view (A) is host/electron-tRPC dependent (local SQLite); empties to friendly text.

### Notes (editor)
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/notes/ (page.tsx -> NotesView from renderer/screens/suite/NotesView). Cloud tRPC (cloudTrpc.notes.*).
- **Состояние:** Fully implemented three-pane workspace (notebooks 200px | notes 240px | reader 1fr) inside SuiteScreen (overridden to max-w-6xl). Left: notebooks list + 'Новый блокнот'. Middle: notes list for active notebook with server FTS search (notes.searchNotes, 280ms debounce, ts_headline snippet highlighting), reorder up/down, move-to-notebook, remove. Right: the note reader. EDITOR COMPONENT = CollaborativeNoteEditor (components/CollaborativeNoteEditor/CollaborativeNoteEditor.tsx). It is gated by ExperimentalFeatureGate featureId 'collaboration.editor': gate CLOSED (default) -> PlainNoteTextarea (a controlled @rox/ui Textarea, min-h-[55vh], font-mono); gate OPEN -> same textarea also bound to a Liveblocks/Yjs CRDT room (noteRoomId(orgId,noteId)) for real-time co-editing. List queries exclude the markdown column; full body fetched via notes.getNote.
- **Gaps:** EDITABLE AFTER CREATE: yes. After createNote succeeds it sets activeNoteId to the new row; the reader then loads notes.getNote and renders CollaborativeNoteEditor keyed by note id, which is a controlled editable Textarea with debounced autosave (notes.updateNote, 800ms) — it does NOT become read-only. Editor remounts per note id (key={noteQuery.data.id}); NotesView hydrates editorMarkdown once per note id (hydratedNoteId ref) so background refetches don't clobber typing, and flushes pending save on unmount/note switch. The create dialog's own markdown Textarea is separate (initial body only). No rich-text/markdown preview — body is a raw markdown textarea only. If collaboration.editor is open but no active org, it silently falls back to single-player (cannot scope a room).

### Mail / Email (width constraint)
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/email/ (page.tsx -> EmailView from renderer/screens/suite/EmailView). Also embeddable in a unified InboxView via controlled props. Cloud tRPC (cloudTrpc.mail.*); bodies fetched from R2.
- **Состояние:** Fully implemented inbox mirroring web: two-pane grid grid-cols-[280px_1fr] (thread list | reader), height h-[calc(100vh-220px)] min-h-96. listThreads (limit 50), getThread for messages, markRead, send (compose dialog). Per-message body fetched from R2 via useMailBody (getBodyUrl html-then-text fallback + plain fetch); HTML sanitized with DOMPurify (sanitizeMailHtml) and injected into an isolated clipped container (max-h-[60vh] overflow-auto), text rendered as escaped pre-wrap. Attachments downloaded via presigned mail.getAttachmentUrl opened in browser. Selection optionally controlled (for InboxView SSE invalidation) else internal.
- **Gaps:** WIDTH CONSTRAINT: the entire mail surface is wrapped by SuiteScreen, whose inner container is `mx-auto w-full max-w-5xl px-6 py-6` (SuiteScreen.tsx). EmailView passes className="max-w-6xl" (EmailView.tsx line 157), so cn() yields BOTH `max-w-5xl` and `max-w-6xl` on the same element — Tailwind class collision; the effective cap depends on stylesheet order (last-defined wins, typically max-w-6xl = 72rem/1152px). Either way the inbox is HARD-CAPPED and centered (mx-auto) and will NOT fill a wide desktop window — left/right gutters appear past ~1152px. NotesView uses the identical pattern (also max-w-6xl). If the desired look is full-width mail, this max-w cap (and the 5xl/6xl class collision) is the thing to change. Additional minor: thread reader column is fixed-template 280px + 1fr, no resize.

### Chat — main workspace ChatPane (legacy/mosaic screen)
- **Entry:** Rendered inside the mosaic tab system at apps/desktop/src/renderer/screens/main/.../TabView/ChatPane/ChatPane.tsx (paneType: "chat"). Not a TanStack route; mounted as a Mosaic pane via the tabs store.
- **Состояние:** Full-featured chat pane. ChatPane wraps ChatRuntimeServiceProvider + ChatServiceProvider (both IPC clients created at module scope) around BasePaneWindow. Toolbar = SessionSelector (switch/new/delete session) + SessionObjectLinkLauncher + split/close actions. Body = ChatPaneInterface: model picker (useAvailableModels: dev models else apiTrpcClient.chat.getModels), thinkingLevel + permissionMode (default 'bypassPermissions'), streaming via useChatDisplay (fps:60), optimistic user turns (pendingUserTurn + toOptimisticUserMessage), file uploads (useOptimisticUpload/uploadFiles), slash commands (useSlashCommandExecutor), MCP controls (useMcpUi), tool/subagent rendering, plan/approval/question response handlers, auto-launch of initialLaunchConfig with retry (max 3, 1500ms), and auto-titling of pane/tab from first submitted message. DraftSaver persists composer drafts per pane.
- **Gaps:** Heavy duplication: this ChatPaneInterface (~1060 lines) is a near-copy of the v2-workspace one but uses the chat-runtime IPC client (session.sendMessage / restartFromMessage / listMessages cache writes) instead of workspaceTrpc, and LACKS the v2 features: no conversation sharing, no custom-provider model discovery, no animated pending-approval band. Two parallel chat stacks must be kept in sync by hand. permissionMode state exists but is hardwired to 'bypassPermissions' and never persisted.

### Chat — v2-workspace ChatPane (current dashboard workspace)
- **Entry:** Route: /_authenticated/_dashboard/v2-workspace/$workspaceId (page.tsx). Chat is one pane type in the pane registry: hooks/usePaneRegistry/components/ChatPane/ChatPane.tsx.
- **Состояние:** The actively-used workspace chat. ChatPane (thin, 51 lines) wraps a single ChatServiceProvider (module-scope IPC client, shared by the ModelPicker's provider-status + custom-provider queries) and renders WorkspaceChatInterface via useWorkspaceChatController (onSessionIdChange/getOrCreateSession/handleNewChat). WorkspaceChatInterface uses workspaceTrpc.chat.* (sendMessage/restartFromMessage/getSlashCommands/getMcpOverview) and useWorkspaceChatDisplay for streaming. Adds over the legacy pane: conversation Share (apiTrpcClient.share.publishChatSession + copy link), live custom-provider model discovery on picker-open (auth.discoverCustomProviderModels merged via resolveSelectableModels — comment notes a freshly discovered 'rox-custom/<id>' selection would otherwise snap back to house model 'ROX R1'), framer-motion animated PendingApprovalMessage band (max-w-[680px]), footerScrollTrigger to scroll on approval/question overlays. Optimistic new-session sends held in pendingUserTurn to survive stale 4fps snapshot polls.
- **Gaps:** Same dual-stack duplication risk as the legacy pane (two ChatInputFooter, ChatMessageList, useMcpUi, useSlashCommandExecutor trees under different paths). Custom-provider model resolution is intricate and comment-flagged as fragile (silent fallback to house model if lookup misses). permissionMode again hardwired to 'bypassPermissions'. ModelPicker is the subject of an open visual task (glass styling) — lives under WorkspaceChatInterface/components/ModelPicker.

### Quick chat
- **Entry:** Route: /_authenticated/_dashboard/quick-chat → QuickChatView. Web twin at apps/web/src/app/(agents)/chat/components/WebQuickChatView.
- **Состояние:** A self-contained, project-less chat. Local useState messages (no harness/streaming), single completion call apiClient.chat.complete.mutate({sessionId, messages, modelId, reasoning}). One lazily-created chat_sessions row per conversation (crypto.randomUUID in sessionIdRef) so the Журнал can summarize it. Model dropdown over AVAILABLE_CHAT_MODELS (default ROX_CHAT_MODEL), reasoning level pills (REASONING_LEVELS, DEFAULT_REASONING_LEVEL). Empty state shows STARTER_PROMPTS chips (subset of DEFAULT_SAVED_PROMPTS via STARTER_PROMPT_IDS) and consumes a staged prompt from useQuickChatDraftStore. Handles three outcomes via resolveQuickChatOutcome: reply, 'notice' (non-house model needs user key → NEEDS_USER_KEY_NOTICE bubble), and house-model not-configured → inline actionable NOT_CONFIGURED_BANNER + CTA to /settings/models, send disabled while active (shouldBlockSend), user text preserved. Full RU localization. Submit on Enter (Shift+Enter newline).
- **Gaps:** No streaming (single awaited mutate; only a '{model} печатает…' spinner). No persisted message history/rehydration — messages live only in component state, lost on unmount/navigation (only the session row + draft persist). No file attachments, no slash commands, no stop/abort, no edit/resend. Generic catch maps every failure to GENERIC_ERROR_NOTICE bubble. scrollRef initial effect has empty deps so only scrolls once on mount.

### Canvas — dashboard route (entity-backed Canvas Workspace)
- **Entry:** Route: /_authenticated/_dashboard/canvas (canvas/page.tsx) → CanvasWorkspaceView. Selects workspace via selectDefaultCanvasWorkspace (last-active localStorage → pinned[0] → all[0]; E2E fixture under E2E_AUTH_BYPASS).
- **Состояние:** Real, persistence-backed canvas. page.tsx resolves a workspace then mounts CanvasWorkspaceView under WorkspaceTrpcProvider (hostUrl from useLocalHostService; shows 'Starting local Canvas workspace...' until activeHostUrl). CanvasWorkspaceView (~1390 lines) wires workspaceTrpc.canvas.* : list/get/getHistory/listCapabilities queries; create/patch/undo/redo/runCapability/importJsonCanvas mutations; auto-creates a 'Production Canvas Workspace' doc when the list is empty; 5s polling refetch (CANVAS_ACTIVE_REFRESH_INTERVAL_MS) with sync-status pill (data-testid=canvas-sync-status). Edits go through CanvasMutationBatch with client-side inverse batches for undo/redo (history capped at 50) plus server undo/redo fallback. JSON Canvas import/export (Obsidian interop) with clipboard copy. Canvas command palette (Cmd/Ctrl+Shift+P) + keyboard shortcuts (undo/redo/export). When a doc+index exist it renders the REAL ReactFlowCanvasAdapter; capability buttons gated by getCanvasCapabilityDisabledReason (needs active canvas / not pending / selection when requiresSelection).
- **Gaps:** Significant placeholder/decorative scaffolding around the real adapter: the left 'Library' list, the 'Entity-backed nodes' chips, the floating toolbar ['Select','Text','Note','Session','Edge','Group'] (static buttons, only index 0 highlighted, no handlers), the 'Zoom 86% · Grid on' readout (hardcoded), and the bottom-right minimap (9 static cells) are all non-functional chrome. When NO active document, it falls back to CanvasNodeCard placeholders + a hand-drawn SVG CanvasConnectionLayer (fake nodes/edges). Capability run results are summarized generically (summarizeCapabilityResult). selectionScopeKey effect resets selectedCanvasId on every scope change (always null branch). Heavy dark glass styling (bg-[#07090f], radial gradients) diverges from the rest of the app's theme.

### Canvas — pipeline editor (Agent Pipelines / PipelineCanvas)
- **Entry:** Route: /_authenticated/_dashboard/pipelines (list) and /_authenticated/_dashboard/pipelines/$pipelineId (editor) → PipelineEditor. The graph canvas is PipelineCanvas (xyflow).
- **Состояние:** Working xyflow-based pipeline editor. PipelineEditor owns the authoritative RoxWorkflowState (graphRef), converts to/from xyflow via graph-adapter (stateToNodes/stateToEdges/flowToState; node kinds: start, agent_run, loop, human_approval, response), debounce-saves edits (800ms) through pipeline.updateGraph, and toggles a right panel between NodeInspector (when a node is selected) and Tabs[Роли|Триггеры|Запуски] (RoleLibraryPanel/TriggerConfigPanel/RunMonitorPanel). ADDING NODES: two paths, both call PipelineEditor.addNode(kind) — (a) the in-canvas xyflow Panel (top-left) with 4 ghost buttons 'Агент/Цикл/Подтверждение/Финал' (PipelineCanvas onAddNode), and (b) RoleLibraryPanel → addRoleNode(roleSlug,label) → addNode('agent_run', roleSlug, label). addNode synthesizes a block id (kind_<rand>), positions it in a cascade, writes subBlocks.roleSlug if given, and auto-selects it to open the inspector. Edges are created by dragging connections (handleConnect → addEdge with animated marker). Toolbar shows a live validity Badge ('граф валиден' vs 'N проблем(ы)') + SaveIndicator. NODE CONFIG: NodeInspector renders an enabled Switch (non-start), a per-block issues list, and a type-specific form. AgentNodeForm is FULLY EDITABLE — role Select (agentRole.list), modelOverride Input, maxTurns (1-200), temperature (0-2), all writing subBlocks via patch.patchNode.
- **Gaps:** VALIDATION SOURCE / STALENESS: PipelineEditor calls validate with ONLY { pipelineId } (validateInput = useMemo {pipelineId}). The server (pipeline.ts validate, lines 127-146) therefore loads the DB-PERSISTED draftState (not the in-memory edited graph) and runs validateGraph (workflow-core: exactly-one-start, edge endpoints exist, no cycles, reachability incl. DISABLED_BRIDGE_BLOCK/UNREACHABLE_BLOCK, unknown-type, skill-input mapping). validate is invalidated only in updateGraph.onSuccess — so the 'N проблем(ы)' badge and the inspector's per-node issues LAG the live canvas by the 800ms debounce + round-trip, and can show stale problems for unsaved edits. WHY NODE CONFIG CAN LOOK DISABLED: (1) the Start node has NO config form — StartNodeForm is just explanatory RU text, and NodeInspector guards the enabled Switch AND the delete button behind !isStart (lines 113, 151), so a selected start node shows zero editable controls; (2) the agent-role Select only lists roles from agentRole.list — if that query is empty/unauthorized you see only 'Без роли' with the hint 'Узел не выполнится без привязанной роли'; (3) the whole inspector is hidden when rolesPanelOpen is false (toggle in toolbar). The numeric inputs also silently no-op on non-finite values. validate query has no explicit enabled gate.

### Mail (Email inbox) — width constraint
- **Entry:** Route: /_authenticated/_dashboard/email (email/page.tsx) → EmailView. Also embeddable (controlled) inside a unified InboxView.
- **Состояние:** Functional 2-pane inbox: thread list (mail.listThreads, limit 50) in a fixed grid-cols-[280px_1fr], thread reader (mail.getThread) on the right, compose/reply Dialog (mail.send), markRead, attachments via presigned mail.getAttachmentUrl (opened in browser). Full body fetched from R2 per message (useMailBody): HTML sanitized with DOMPurify (sanitizeMailHtml) into an isolated clipped container (max-h-[60vh], [&_img]:max-w-full); text rendered escaped; snippet is the loading/error fallback. Cache-first. RU localized ('Почта', 'Написать', 'Входящих нет').
- **Gaps:** WIDTH CONSTRAINT: the whole view is wrapped in SuiteScreen with className="max-w-6xl" (EmailView.tsx line 157) — so on wide desktop windows the inbox is capped at ~72rem (max-w-6xl) and centered, leaving large empty side gutters rather than filling the workspace. Inner content area is also fixed-height grid h-[calc(100vh-220px)] min-h-96 with a hardcoded 280px thread-list column. SuiteScreen is the shared wrapper (same max-w-6xl cap as NotesView). Body fetch is per-message and eager (useMailBody(messageId, true)) for every rendered message.

### Notes — editor component & post-create editability
- **Entry:** Route: /_authenticated/_dashboard/notes (notes/page.tsx) → NotesView. Editor: NotesView/components/CollaborativeNoteEditor.
- **Состояние:** Three-pane notes workspace (notebooks 200px | notes 240px | reader 1fr) under SuiteScreen. Notebooks (notes.listNotebooks, auto-select first), notes (notes.listNotes, body column excluded), per-note body fetched via notes.getNote. Server FTS search (notes.searchNotes, debounced 280ms) with highlighted snippets. Create-notebook and create-note dialogs (title + markdown). Notebook membership management: move between notebooks, remove, reorder up/down (reorderNotebookItems, optimistic). EDITOR = CollaborativeNoteEditor (keyed by note id): wrapped in ExperimentalFeatureGate featureId='collaboration.editor'. Gate CLOSED (default) → PlainNoteTextarea (controlled Textarea, min-h-[55vh], autosave via parent handleEditorChange → notes.updateNote on 800ms debounce, with unmount/note-switch flush). Gate OPEN AND an active org present → YjsNoteTextarea: same textarea bound to a shared Y.Doc over the existing note Liveblocks room (noteRoomId(org,note)), token via collab.authRoom, real-time co-editing with 'Совместное редактирование: N участника' indicator; no org → falls back to plain textarea.
- **Gaps:** EDITABILITY AFTER CREATE: YES — after createNote.onSuccess sets activeNoteId, the reader pane mounts the editable CollaborativeNoteEditor and STAYS editable (autosave continues); it is not a read-only viewer. The note title shown in the reader header is NOT editable inline (only the body markdown is; title is set only in the create dialog) — no rename-note affordance anywhere in NotesView. The create-note dialog's markdown Textarea is separate from the editor and only used for initial body. Collaborative editing is feature-gated OFF by default, so most users get single-player autosave only. Same SuiteScreen max-w-6xl width cap as Mail. Autosave debounce captures targetNoteId at schedule time to avoid cross-note writes (good), but a very fast create→type→navigate could still rely on the unmount flush.

### Notes
- **Entry:** Route /_authenticated/_dashboard/notes/ -> apps/desktop/src/renderer/routes/_authenticated/_dashboard/notes/page.tsx (thin wrapper) -> NotesView
- **Состояние:** Three-pane workspace inside SuiteScreen (title 'Заметки', icon BookText, overrides width to max-w-6xl). grid-cols-[200px_240px_1fr] (NotesView.tsx:366): notebooks column | notes column (with server FTS search via notes.searchNotes, debounced 280ms, + reorder up/down + move-to-notebook dropdown + remove) | note reader/editor. Data via tRPC notes.* (listNotebooks/listNotes/getNote/searchNotes/createNotebook/createNote/updateNote/addNoteToNotebook/removeNoteFromNotebook/reorderNotebookItems). List queries exclude the markdown column; full body fetched per-note via getNote. Auto-selects first notebook; create-notebook and create-note dialogs both set the active id so the new item opens immediately. EDITOR COMPONENT: CollaborativeNoteEditor. It is editable after create: the reader pane is an always-editable controlled <Textarea> (PlainNoteTextarea, min-h-[55vh], font-mono) with debounced autosave (AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS=800) through notes.updateNote, plus a flush-on-unmount/note-switch. CollaborativeNoteEditor wraps it in ExperimentalFeatureGate featureId='collaboration.editor': gate CLOSED (the default, since enabled&&availability==='available' is false) -> renders the plain single-player autosave textarea (no regression); gate OPEN -> same textarea is also a Yjs/Liveblocks CRDT peer over room org:{orgId}:note:{noteId}. Editor is keyed by note id so it re-seeds per note; hydration guarded by hydratedNoteId ref so background refetch never clobbers typing.
- **Gaps:** Note BODY is a raw markdown <Textarea> only — no rich-text/markdown WYSIWYG or live preview anywhere (reader pane shows the same editable textarea, never rendered markdown). Title is read-only after create (rename of an existing note's title is not exposed; only body autosaves). No delete-note and no delete-notebook (only move/remove-from-notebook edges; the note document itself can't be deleted from this UI). Collaborative co-editing is gated off by default, so presence/'N участника' indicator is normally invisible. Reorder is one-step up/down buttons only (no drag). Search is scoped to the active notebook only (cannot search across all notebooks).

### Mail (email)
- **Entry:** Route /_authenticated/_dashboard/email/ -> apps/desktop/src/renderer/routes/_authenticated/_dashboard/email/page.tsx (thin wrapper) -> EmailView. ALSO embedded as the 'Почта' transport tab inside InboxView.
- **Состояние:** Two-pane mail client inside SuiteScreen (title 'Почта', icon Mail). Thread list (grid-cols-[280px_1fr], EmailView.tsx:190) via mail.listThreads({limit:50}); right pane = selected thread's messages via mail.getThread. Compose/reply dialog via mail.send (to/subject/body, recipients split on [,;\s]); markRead via mail.markRead with a 'Прочитано' button + unread dot. Per-message full body fetched from R2 via useMailBody (mail.getBodyUrl, HTML-variant-first then text fallback, plain fetch of presigned URL); HTML sanitized with DOMPurify in sanitizeMailHtml (FORBID_TAGS style/form/input/button/textarea/select, FORBID_ATTR style/class/srcset, links hardened to target=_blank rel=noopener) then injected via dangerouslySetInnerHTML into an isolated container 'mail-html-body max-h-[60vh] overflow-auto'; text body rendered as escaped plain text; snippet is the loading/error fallback. Attachments via mail.getMessage (enabled only when hasAttachments) + presigned mail.getAttachmentUrl opened in browser. Selection is optionally controlled (activeThreadId/onSelectThread props) so InboxView can lift it for SSE.
- **Gaps:** WIDTH CONSTRAINT: EmailView renders inside SuiteScreen, whose inner wrapper is 'mx-auto w-full max-w-5xl' (SuiteScreen.tsx:31); EmailView overrides via className='max-w-6xl' (EmailView.tsx:157). So the whole mail UI — thread list + reader — is centered and capped at max-w-6xl (~72rem) with mx-auto, NOT full-bleed; on a wide desktop window there is empty gutter on both sides and the reader pane never uses full width. (When mounted in InboxView's mail tab it is the same EmailView, so the same max-w-6xl cap applies.) Other gaps: no reply/forward/compose-prefill from an open thread (compose is blank-only; the per-message header has no reply action); no delete/archive/move; no folders/labels/search over mail; read receipts one-directional; attachments list only appears after the extra getMessage round-trip.

### Drive
- **Entry:** Route /_authenticated/_dashboard/drive/ -> apps/desktop/src/renderer/routes/_authenticated/_dashboard/drive/page.tsx (thin wrapper) -> DriveView
- **Состояние:** Folder/file browser inside SuiteScreen (title 'Drive', icon HardDrive, default max-w-5xl — no width override). Breadcrumb trail state (trail: Crumb[]); current folder via drive.listFolder({folderId}); rows are a single bordered list of folders (click to drill in via openFolder) then files (with formatFileSize). Create folder via drive.createFolder (dialog + Enter-to-submit). Share link via drive.createShare for a file or folder -> builds https://rox.one/d/<token>, copies to clipboard, shows a read-only share dialog. Empty/loading/error states all handled (skeleton, dashed empty card, SuiteQueryError with retry).
- **Gaps:** P0 surface, intentionally minimal: NO file upload, NO download of files (only share-link creation — comment at DriveView.tsx:43 states 'P0 surfaces share-link creation only'), NO file open/preview, NO rename, NO delete/move, NO folder-share vs file-share distinction in UI beyond the icon, NO drag-and-drop. Files appear but are inert except for the share button. Share link has no expiry/permission controls (dialog text just says 'anyone with the link'). Width capped at max-w-5xl centered (not full width).

### Calendar
- **Entry:** Route /_authenticated/_dashboard/calendar/ -> apps/desktop/src/renderer/routes/_authenticated/_dashboard/calendar/page.tsx (thin wrapper) -> CalendarView
- **Состояние:** Month AGENDA list (not a grid calendar) inside SuiteScreen (title 'Календарь', icon CalendarDays, default max-w-5xl). Reads calendar.listOccurrences for the visible month (monthRange(anchor)); groups expanded occurrences by local day (dayKey) into day-heading sections of event rows. Prev/next month nav re-queries. Clicking a row opens a detail Dialog with per-occurrence overrides (title/desc/location/allDay/time win over series), RSVP buttons (accepted/tentative/declined) via calendar.rsvp, and for recurring events a 'Удалить только это событие' via calendar.cancelOccurrence (passes RECURRENCE-ID originalStart). EventReminders sub-component: list + add-preset (0/10/60/1440 min, in_app) + delete via calendar.listReminders/createReminder/deleteReminder. Owner-only SubscribeFeedDialog (public ICS feed toggle) gated on firstCalendar.ownerUserId===currentUserId. 'truncated' banner when recurrence expansion overflowed the window.
- **Gaps:** Read/RSVP-only — there is NO create-event and NO edit-event UI (comment at CalendarView.tsx:447 'RSVP screen has no full editor'); you cannot add an event from the desktop app, only RSVP/cancel-instance/set reminders. No month-grid or week/day views (agenda list only). No timezone display/control. Reminder channel is hardcoded in_app for new reminders (email channel only shown for pre-existing rows). SubscribeFeedDialog only appears for the owner of the FIRST calendar (calendarsQuery.data[0]); multi-calendar management is absent. Width capped at max-w-5xl centered.

### Inbox
- **Entry:** Route /_authenticated/_dashboard/inbox/ -> apps/desktop/src/renderer/routes/_authenticated/_dashboard/inbox/page.tsx (thin wrapper) -> InboxView
- **Состояние:** Unified inbox with a transport switch (TransportTabs: 'Чат' | 'Почта'). CHAT tab (ChatTab): split-pane (grid-cols-[280px_1fr]) over comms.* — comms.listThreads (with unreadCount badges) | comms.getThread messages + bubble UI (own=right primary, others=left muted) + composer (comms.sendMessage, Enter-to-send, recipients = other participants' userIds). Edit/delete own messages via comms.editMessage/deleteMessage using window.prompt/window.confirm; tombstone 'Сообщение удалено'; auto-scroll to newest. Typing presence via ThreadPresence (Liveblocks, throttled, TYPING_IDLE_MS=2500). MAIL tab: reuses EmailView (same component as /email). Open-thread selection for both transports is lifted into InboxView (chatThreadId/mailThreadId) and fed to useCommsStream (SSE) so a live message/email lands as an invalidate-only refetch of the on-screen thread (cache-first, no row blanking).
- **Gaps:** Edit-message UX uses raw window.prompt() and delete uses window.confirm() (InboxView.tsx:184/191) — not in-app dialogs, jarring on desktop. Chat reply requires >=1 other participant (recipientUserIds) so a solo/self thread can't be replied to (canSend false). No new-conversation / new-recipient compose in the chat tab (can only reply within existing threads). The chat split-pane height is h-[calc(100vh-260px)] (different from the suite default -220px), a magic offset that can mis-size. When switching to the mail tab, InboxView renders EmailView which brings its OWN SuiteScreen header (so the page shows a second 'Почта' header below the transport tabs, and inherits EmailView's max-w-6xl centering). No unified/cross-transport thread list — it's a hard tab switch, not a merged inbox.

### Pipeline editor (asked-for detail)
- **Entry:** Route /_authenticated/_dashboard/pipelines/$pipelineId/ -> apps/desktop/.../pipelines/$pipelineId/page.tsx (loads pipeline.get over cloud tRPC, gates on loading/error) -> PipelineEditor. List at /pipelines -> page.tsx -> PipelinesIndex/PipelinesEmptyState.
- **Состояние:** xyflow (@rox/ui/ai-elements/flow) canvas (PipelineCanvas) wrapped in ReactFlowProvider, plus a right aside that is EITHER the NodeInspector (when a node is selected) OR a 3-tab panel (Роли/Триггеры/Запуски: RoleLibraryPanel/TriggerConfigPanel/RunMonitorPanel). PipelineEditor owns the working RoxWorkflowState (seeded from pipeline.draftState), derives nodes/edges via graph-adapter (stateToNodes/stateToEdges), and debounce-saves (SAVE_DEBOUNCE_MS=800) via pipeline.updateGraph with a single-flight queue + flush-on-unmount; SaveIndicator shows saving/saved. HOW NODES ARE ADDED: (1) Canvas top-left Panel has four ghost '+' buttons — Агент(agent_run)/Цикл(loop)/Подтверждение(human_approval)/Финал(response) — calling onAddNode(kind) (PipelineCanvas.tsx:176-212). (2) RoleLibraryPanel rows call onAddRole(slug,name) -> addRoleNode -> addNode('agent_run', roleSlug, label). addNode (PipelineEditor.tsx:186) creates a block id (kind_xxxxxx), inserts into graph.blocks with a cascade position and subBlocks.roleSlug, persists, and auto-selects the new node so the inspector opens. Edges added by dragging handles -> onConnect -> addEdge (animated, ArrowClosed). WHERE VALIDATION/PROBLEMS COME FROM: server-side query trpc.pipeline.validate({pipelineId}) (PipelineEditor.tsx:126), re-invalidated after every updateGraph save (onSuccess line 103). Toolbar badge reads validation.valid ? 'граф валиден' : `${validation.issues.length} проблем(ы)` (line 246-255). Per-node problems: NodeInspector filters validation.issues to issue.blockId===blockId (NodeInspector.tsx:76) and lists issue.message in a 'Проблемы узла' box. Issue type = WorkflowIssue from @rox/workflow-core. NODE CONFIG (role/steps/model): NodeInspector header (icon + InlineRename + 'Узел включён' Switch[patch.enabled] + delete) and a per-kind sub-form. AgentNodeForm fields: 'Роль агента' Select populated by agentRole.list (writes subBlocks.roleSlug, sentinel __none__ = 'Без роли'); 'Модель (переопределение)' free-text Input -> subBlocks.modelOverride; 'Макс. шагов' number 1-200 -> subBlocks.maxTurns; 'Температура' number 0-2 -> subBlocks.temperature. All writes go through useNodePatch -> buildNodePatch (pure) -> applyGraphChange (same debounced save).
- **Gaps:** WHY NODE CONFIG (role/steps/model) MIGHT APPEAR DISABLED/UNAVAILABLE — grounded findings: there is NO static `disabled`/`readOnly`/`pointer-events-none`/feature-gate on any node-config field (verified by rg across the pipelines dir; the only `disabled` hits are pending-mutation BUTTON guards in PipelinesIndex/RoleLibraryPanel/TriggerConfigPanel/RunMonitorPanel/PipelineTemplateCard). So the fields are never code-disabled. Instead the config is INACCESSIBLE/EMPTY in these cases: (a) NodeInspector only renders when rolesPanelOpen===true AND selectedNode!=null (PipelineEditor.tsx:293-302) — if the right panel is collapsed via the PanelRightClose toggle, ALL node config is hidden (looks like there's no config). (b) The 'Роль агента' dropdown only lists roles returned by agentRole.list; with no seeded roles it shows just 'Без роли' (+ the static ROLE_TEMPLATES in RoleLibraryPanel, but the Select in AgentNodeForm does NOT include templates) — so role selection can look empty until agentRole.seedBuiltins is run. (c) MODEL is a free-text Input (placeholder 'напр. gpt-5'), NOT a model-picker dropdown — there is no curated model list, so 'model selection' is just a string field (easy to read as 'no model picker'/disabled). (d) StartNodeForm renders only explanatory text (start node has no editable body and cannot be deleted; rename only via header) — the inspector body for a start node is intentionally empty. (e) For a node bound to a slug not in agentRole.list, AgentNodeForm shows an amber 'Роль не найдена' hint (still editable). Other editor gaps: TriggerConfigPanel passes selectedNodeLabel={null} hardcoded (PipelineEditor.tsx:329); loop-body membership is NOT editable (LoopNodeForm comment: 'настраивается связями на холсте', v1); no run trigger from the editor toolbar (run lives in RunMonitorPanel tab); deleting the sole start block is refused (buildNodeDelete start_protected).

### Memory (Память)
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/memory/ → page.tsx renders <MemoryView/> from renderer/screens/memory/MemoryView. Sidebar/topbar from _dashboard/layout.tsx.
- **Состояние:** Functional and data-backed. Centered single column (max-w-3xl, px-6 py-8), RU header 'Память'. Data via TanStack-DB live query over collections.memoryItems filtered by createdBy=userId (Electric-synced, optimistic). Three regions: (1) ImportPanel — collapsible 'Импорт памяти из других AI' with two real mechanisms: copyable export prompt + paste box (apiClient.memory.submitPromptImport) and conversations.json archive upload up to 8MB (apiClient.memory.startArchiveImport, ChatGPT/Anthropic), with live job-status line driven by collections.memoryImportJobs. (2) MemorySuggestions — status='suggested' items with inline Принять/Отклонить that update status to approved/dismissed optimistically; renders nothing when none pending. (3) MEMORY_GROUPS categories (from groups.ts), each MemoryGroup shows approved items (delete on hover via collections.memoryItems.delete), non-persisted seed examples with 'Добавить себе' when category empty+ready, and a freehand Input that inserts a manual approved memory on Enter. Writes go through Electric collection onInsert/onDelete → memory tRPC router.
- **Gaps:** All gating depends on session.user.id AND session.activeOrganizationId being present; if either is empty, insertMemory silently no-ops (no toast, button still appears) and examples are hidden — a dev/local-only or org-less session shows an inert add box. No edit-in-place for an existing memory (only add + delete). Suggested items only ever appear if an agent/import populates status='suggested'; with no backend producing them the Suggestions banner is permanently absent. ImportPanel mechanisms hit the cloud apiClient — fail with generic toasts if cloud unreachable. Comment in MemoryView calls suggestions 'phase 3', implying agent-side suggestion production may not be wired end-to-end yet.

### Journal (Журнал)
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/journal/ → page.tsx renders <JournalView/> from renderer/screens/journal/JournalView.
- **Состояние:** Read-only viewer, data-backed. Centered column (max-w-3xl), RU header 'Журнал'. Two tabs via @rox/ui/tabs: 'Рефлексия' (defaultValue='reflection') and 'Лента' ('feed'). Both lanes are TanStack-DB live queries filtered by createdBy=userId: lane 1 collections.journalEntries (once-daily reflection, sorted newest day first, rendered as JournalDay), lane 2 collections.journalEvents (continuous event stream, sorted newest-first, rendered as JournalFeed). Cache-first: skeletons (ReflectionSkeleton/FeedSkeleton) only when zero rows AND collection not ready; otherwise renders rows immediately. Empty reflection shows 'Журнал пока пуст' with copy explaining 'Rox R1 разбирает твои сессии' daily.
- **Gaps:** Purely consumptive — there is NO create/edit/delete UI in the journal; entries/events are expected to be produced by a background agent (R1) writing to the Electric collections. If nothing populates journal_entries/journal_events, the Reflection tab sits on the empty state and the Feed tab renders an empty JournalFeed forever. FeedLane has no dedicated empty-state component (only skeleton vs JournalFeed), so a ready-but-empty feed depends on JournalFeed's own internal handling. No date filtering/search/pagination — entire user history is loaded client-side and sorted in-memory.

### Skills library (Библиотека скиллов)
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/skills-library/ → page.tsx renders <SkillsLibraryView/> (route-local component).
- **Состояние:** Functional, local-filesystem backed via electronTrpc (main-process tRPC, NOT cloud). Two-pane: left aside w-80 with header 'Библиотека скиллов', a search Input (client-side filter over name/slug/description), and a scroll list of skills from electronTrpc.skillsLibrary.list (staleTime 30s). Each row shows name, a mono source badge mapped via SOURCE_LABELS ({claude:'~/.claude', agents:'~/.agents'}, else raw source), and 2-line description. Right section: SkillDetailPane (keyed by skill id) for the selected skill, else an Empty state 'Выберите скилл'. SkillDetailPane loads electronTrpc.skillsLibrary.get, defaults active file to SKILL.md (or first file), shows header (name/description/absolutePath), a w-56 file list, and an editable mono Textarea bound to electronTrpc.skillsLibrary.readFile; Save button (disabled unless dirty) writes via skillsLibrary.writeFile and invalidates caches; success toast 'Файл скилла сохранён'.
- **Gaps:** Reads/writes the user's real local skill dirs on disk — only ~/.claude and ~/.agents have friendly labels; any other source shows the raw source string. No create/delete/rename of skills or files (edit existing file contents only). No frontmatter/markdown preview — raw text editor only. No dirty-guard on switching files or selecting another skill (unsaved Textarea edits to draft are silently dropped on navigation since draft re-seeds from fileData per file). Save has no per-file conflict detection. Entirely dependent on the desktop main process exposing skillsLibrary.* (electron-only) — would be empty/non-functional in any web build.

### Saved prompts (Сохранённые промпты)
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/saved-prompts/ → page.tsx renders <SavedPromptsView/> (route-local).
- **Состояние:** Fully functional CRUD, local-DB backed via electronTrpc.savedPrompts (SelectSavedPrompt from @rox/local-db — local SQLite, not cloud). Full-width flex column: header 'Сохранённые промпты' + 'Новый промпт' button. List via savedPrompts.list.useQuery, centered ul max-w-3xl. Empty state shows DEFAULT_SAVED_PROMPTS examples (dashed cards) each with 'Сохранить' (create from example), insert-in-chat, and copy. Saved rows show title + 3-line body, hover actions: Вставить в чат (stagePrompt via useQuickChatDraftStore then navigate to /quick-chat), Скопировать (useCopyToClipboard), Редактировать (opens edit dialog), Удалить (savedPrompts.delete). Create/Edit share a Dialog with title Input (maxLength 200) + body Textarea; handleSubmit validates non-empty title+body, routes to create or update mutation; success/error toasts. DialogState is a discriminated union (closed/create/edit).
- **Gaps:** Local-only persistence (electronTrpc/local SQLite) — prompts do NOT sync across devices or to cloud; desktop-only surface. Delete is immediate with NO confirmation dialog (single click destroys a prompt). No search/filter, no folders/tags, no ordering (relies on default list order from the query). No dedupe — saving the same example twice creates duplicates. 'Вставить в чат' hard-navigates to /quick-chat and depends on the quick-chat-draft store contract.

### Settings (Настройки)
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/settings (sibling of _dashboard, NOT under it). settings/page.tsx redirects to /settings/account. settings/layout.tsx is the chrome (own titlebar + SettingsSidebar + animated Outlet).
- **Состояние:** Mature, broad multi-section settings shell. layout.tsx: full-screen (h-screen w-screen bg-tertiary), custom draggable titlebar (mac left-pad 96px) with NavigationControls, then SettingsSidebar (w-56: back-link to originRoute, title 'Настройки', search input, GeneralSettings nav list, footer doc links Навыки/MCP/Документация) + content area (m-3 rounded, max-w-7xl unless projects/hosts/agents which use inner sidebar via Outlet). Global settings search (settings-search.ts) filters/auto-navigates to first section with matches; SearchResultsBanner shown when active. ~30 section routes exist: account, appearance, ringtones, keyboard, behavior, git, terminal, links, shares, models, organization, teams, members, integrations, api-keys, permissions, hosts/$hostId, network-filter, security, voice (+VoiceHistory), experimental, presets, projects/project/$projectId (incl cloud/secrets), v2-project/$projectId. Escape key navigates up one level or back to origin. Section transitions use framer-motion opacity fade gated by useShouldAnimate('decorative').
- **Gaps:** SECTION_ORDER in layout.tsx (used for search auto-nav) omits several sections that have routes — members, network-filter, security, voice, presets, projects are NOT in SECTION_ORDER, so settings-search auto-navigation can't land on them. getSectionFromPath/getPathFromSection also don't map members/security/voice/network-filter/ringtones-vs-order edge cases consistently with the sidebar. Sidebar visibility is gated by useIsV2CloudEnabled (getVisibleMatchCountBySection) — some sections only show under V2 cloud. AccountSettings (default landing) gates each block via isItemVisible/settings-search visibleItems and mixes session (better-auth) + Electric users collection; falls back to session user when org member row absent (per cache-first comment). Heavy reliance on activeOrganization for org/teams/members/integrations sections.

### Pipeline editor (Пайплайны агентов) — DEEP DIVE
- **Entry:** Index: /_authenticated/_dashboard/pipelines/ → <PipelinesIndex/>. Editor: /_authenticated/_dashboard/pipelines/$pipelineId/ → page loads cloudTrpc.pipeline.get then renders <PipelineEditor/>. Cloud (Neon) data over cloud tRPC, NOT Electric/local.
- **Состояние:** xyflow (@rox/ui/ai-elements/flow) canvas editor over a RoxWorkflowState graph (jsonb workflow_definitions.draftState, engine='pipeline'). NODES ADDED two ways, both call PipelineEditor.addNode(kind, roleSlug?, label?): (1) the canvas top-left <Panel> has 4 ghost buttons 'Агент/Цикл/Подтверждение/Финал' → onAddNode(kind) with no role; (2) the right-panel RoleLibraryPanel rows ('+') call onAddRole(slug,name) → addNode('agent_run', slug, name). addNode mints id `${kind}_${rand}`, positions it in a cascade by block count, sets subBlocks.roleSlug if provided, applies to graph, and auto-selects it (opens inspector). Edges created by dragging handles (handleConnect→addEdge, animated). Node drag/remove persist via handleNodesChange (structural changes only). Persistence: applyGraphChange → debounced 800ms pipeline.updateGraph; SaveIndicator shows сохранение…/сохранено. VALIDATION/PROBLEMS: PipelineEditor runs validateQuery = cloud pipeline.validate (re-run on every successful save via query invalidation). Server pipeline.validate → validateGraph() in @rox/workflow-core, which accumulates issues: MISSING/MULTIPLE_START_BLOCK, INVALID_EDGE_SOURCE/TARGET, CYCLE_DETECTED, UNREACHABLE_BLOCK, DISABLED_BRIDGE_BLOCK, UNKNOWN_BLOCK_TYPE (strict only), skill input-mapping issues. Toolbar shows a 'граф валиден' or 'N проблем(ы)' Badge; NodeInspector filters issues by issue.blockId and renders a per-node 'Проблемы узла' list. NODE CONFIG (right panel): when a node is selected AND rolesPanelOpen, the aside shows NodeInspector instead of the Roles/Triggers/Runs tabs. Inspector header = type icon + inline rename + (non-start) 'Узел включён' Switch + close; body = type sub-form. AgentNodeForm: Role Select (agentRole.list), free-text Model override Input, Макс. шагов (1–200) and Температура (0–2) number Inputs — ALL writes go via patch.patchNode→subBlocksPatch/deleteSubBlockKeys, folded into the same debounced save (useNodePatch reads graphRef so drags aren't clobbered).
- **Gaps:** WHY NODE CONFIG CAN APPEAR DISABLED/UNUSABLE (none are statically disabled in code — every AgentNodeForm input is editable): (1) The inspector ONLY renders when a node is selected AND rolesPanelOpen=true; the toolbar PanelRightClose toggle can hide the whole panel (defaults open), so after collapsing it the per-node config is simply not shown. (2) StartNodeForm is intentionally a static helper paragraph with NO editable fields and NO enabled-Switch/delete (start is singular and undeletable) — selecting the Start node looks like 'config disabled'. (3) The Role <Select> is populated ONLY from cloud agentRole.list; with no org roles and an empty roles array the dropdown contains just 'Без роли' + the static ROLE_TEMPLATES rows in RoleLibraryPanel — if cloud tRPC/active-org is unreachable (requireActiveOrgMembership), agentRole.list errors and the Select shows only 'Без роли', so an agent node can't bind a real role and shows 'Узел не выполнится без привязанной роли'. (4) The 'Узел включён' Switch can disable a node; a disabled node still has fully editable config (no greying), but validateGraph will flag downstream nodes (DISABLED_BRIDGE_BLOCK) — easy to misread as 'config broken'. (5) Entire editor depends on cloud pipeline.get/validate/updateGraph + agentRole.list — on a local-only/offline desktop session these hang or error: validate Badge never appears, saves toast 'Не удалось сохранить граф', and the role library is empty. (6) TriggerConfigPanel is mounted with selectedNodeLabel={null} hardcoded. (7) No explicit run button visible in PipelineEditor.tsx (runOnce exists server-side); run monitoring is a separate RunMonitorPanel tab. (8) graph-adapter coerces any unknown block type to 'agent_run' for rendering, so non-standard persisted blocks silently appear as agent nodes.

### Notes editor (Заметки) — editor component + post-create editability
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/notes/ → page.tsx renders <NotesView/> from renderer/screens/suite/NotesView. Editor component = CollaborativeNoteEditor.
- **Состояние:** Three-pane SuiteScreen (title 'Заметки', className='max-w-6xl', actions 'Новый блокнот'): notebooks (200px) | notes list+search (240px) | note reader (1fr), grid h-[calc(100vh-220px)]. Cloud tRPC (useCloudTrpc). Notebooks via notes.listNotebooks; notes via notes.listNotes (excludes the markdown column); server FTS via notes.searchNotes (debounced 280ms, scoped to active notebook). Editor component is CollaborativeNoteEditor: behind ExperimentalFeatureGate featureId='collaboration.editor' — gate CLOSED (default) renders PlainNoteTextarea (a controlled mono Textarea, min-h-55vh); gate OPEN renders a Yjs/Liveblocks CRDT-bound textarea (RoomProvider + createNoteYjsBinding, token via collab.authRoom) that converges with web peers and shows 'Совместное редактирование: N участника'. EDITABILITY AFTER CREATE: YES — fully editable. createNote (notes.createNote) on success sets activeNoteId to the new row; the reader pane immediately mounts CollaborativeNoteEditor keyed by note id. NotesView hydrates editorMarkdown from notes.getNote once per note id (hydratedNoteId ref, so background refetch never clobbers typing) and AUTOSAVES via notes.updateNote on an 800ms debounce, capturing the note id at schedule time, with an unmount/note-switch flush so the last edit is never dropped. Reader header shows 'Сохранение…' while updateNote.isPending. Also supports notebook membership ops: move note between notebooks, remove from notebook, reorder (up/down, optimistic).
- **Gaps:** The editor is a raw markdown Textarea — no rich-text/markdown preview/toolbar; the create-note dialog body is likewise a plain Textarea. Editing happens directly on the active note via debounced autosave (no explicit Save button, no dirty indicator beyond the transient 'Сохранение…'). Title is NOT editable after create (header shows noteQuery.data.title read-only; only the body autosaves). Collaboration requires an active organization id; with none, CollaborativeNoteEditorInner falls back to single-player even if the gate is open. Reorder/move depend on note.knowledgeDocumentId being non-null (canManage=false otherwise → buttons disabled). Whole surface is cloud-dependent; offline shows query errors. No delete-note action in the list (only move/remove-from-notebook).

### Mail (Почта) — width constraint
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/email/ region → EmailView from renderer/screens/suite/EmailView (also embedded by InboxView). Standalone mounts with no props (internal selection).
- **Состояние:** Mirrors web inbox: thread list (mail.listThreads, limit 50) + thread reader (mail.getThread); compose/reply via mail.send; read-state via mail.markRead. Bodies fetched per-message from R2 via useMailBody; HTML sanitized with DOMPurify (sanitizeMailHtml) into an isolated clipped container (max-h-60vh), text rendered escaped; snippet is the fallback. Attachments via presigned mail.getAttachmentUrl opened in browser. WIDTH CONSTRAINT: EmailView wraps everything in <SuiteScreen className="max-w-6xl">. SuiteScreen's inner column is `mx-auto w-full max-w-5xl px-6 py-6`, and cn() (tailwind-merge) lets the passed `max-w-6xl` OVERRIDE the default `max-w-5xl`. Net: the entire mail UI (header + the grid) is capped at max-w-6xl (~72rem/1152px) and centered with mx-auto. The thread area itself is grid-cols-[280px_1fr] with fixed height h-[calc(100vh-220px)] min-h-96.
- **Gaps:** On a wide desktop window the mail view does NOT fill the viewport width — it is hard-capped at max-w-6xl and centered, leaving large empty gutters on big screens. The cap comes from SuiteScreen's max-width container, overridden per-view to 6xl (Notes uses the same 6xl; other suite screens default to 5xl). Anyone expecting a full-width two-pane mail client will see the constrained centered column. The thread list column is a fixed 280px regardless of width. Reader height is viewport-locked (calc(100vh-220px)) which can mismatch the actual dashboard chrome height. To make mail full-width the SuiteScreen max-width wrapper (or this view's use of it) must change.

### App window layout + shell (TanStack Router shell, NOT screens/main as primary)
- **Entry:** renderer/routes/__root.tsx -> /_authenticated/layout.tsx -> /_authenticated/_dashboard/layout.tsx (Outlet). AppFrame in screens/main is a thin legacy wrapper.
- **Состояние:** The real shell is the router: _authenticated/layout.tsx mounts WallpaperBackground + Outlet inside DnD/Collections/WorkerPool providers; _dashboard/layout.tsx is the visible window chrome: a flex row of [optional WorkspaceSidebar via ResizablePanel] + [column: <TopBar/> + <Outlet/> wrapped in RouteTransition] + a fixed `#workspace-right-sidebar-slot`. Whole shell is `flex h-full w-full overflow-hidden` with framer-motion shellBootVariants entrance. globals.css pins html/body/app to 100vw/100vh, overflow:hidden, user-select:none, 12px base font. There is a hard V1/V2 fork: useIsV2CloudEnabled() chooses DashboardSidebar(v2) vs WorkspaceSidebar(v1), and routes /workspace/$id (v1, screens/main ContentView) vs /v2-workspace/$id (v2, usePaneRegistry).
- **Gaps:** AppFrame.tsx (screens/main) is essentially dead: it renders `absolute inset-0 bg-background flex` but the live shell is the router layout. Background.tsx renders a hardcoded blue/purple `linear-gradient(135deg,#8B9DC3...)` + SVG noise filter that is NOT wired into the authenticated shell (only WallpaperBackground is mounted) — likely orphaned/legacy. The dual V1/V2 surface duplication (two ChatPaneInterface, two ChatComposerControls, two ThinkingMessage trees) is a maintenance hazard: fixes must be applied twice.

### Content padding + max-width (chat reading column)
- **Entry:** V1: /workspace/$workspaceId -> ContentView -> TabsContent -> ChatPane/ChatPaneInterface. V2: /v2-workspace/$workspaceId -> usePaneRegistry ChatPane/WorkspaceChatInterface/ChatPaneInterface.
- **Состояние:** ContentView is `h-full flex flex-col overflow-hidden`: ContentHeader (h-10, GroupStrip) + optional PresetsBar + TabsContent. V2 chat wrapper is `flex h-full w-full flex-col bg-background` and its message column is centered at `mx-auto w-full max-w-[680px] px-4`. V1 ChatPaneInterface root is just `flex h-full flex-col bg-background` (line 996) — the inner message list/composer set their own widths. Suite screens (Notes/Mail/Drive/Calendar) center content via SuiteScreen `mx-auto w-full max-w-5xl px-6 py-6`.
- **Gaps:** Inconsistent reading-column widths across surfaces: V2 chat is 680px, Suite is max-w-5xl(1024px), mail/notes override to max-w-6xl. V1 chat root has no max-width/centering at its top level (relies on descendants), so V1 vs V2 chat padding/measure can visibly differ. No shared layout token for content max-width — each surface hardcodes its own.

### Preset bar + pane open order
- **Entry:** ContentView renders <PresetsBar/> when settings.getShowPresetsBar is true (between ContentHeader and TabsContent).
- **Состояние:** PresetsBar is `flex items-center h-8 border-b border-border bg-background px-2 gap-0.5 overflow-x-auto`: a gear DropdownMenu (Manage Presets: lists AGENT_TYPES templates + custom presets, pin/unpin via LuPin, 'Show Preset Bar' checkbox, 'Управление пресетами' -> /settings/terminal), a divider, then pinned PresetBarItem chips (icon via getPresetIcon/isDark), and a right-aligned WorkspaceRunButton. Pinned order is locally reorderable (drag) and persisted via reorderPresets. PresetBarItem left-click = onOpenDefault (target active-tab); context menu = Open in current terminal / Open in current tab (split-pane override) / Open in new tab / Edit. preset-launch.ts resolveLaunchPlan maps (target x mode x command count) into: active-tab-single, active-tab-multi-pane, new-tab-single, new-tab-multi-pane, new-tab-per-command. Multiple commands in a preset open as multiple panes (multi-pane) or per-command new tabs.
- **Gaps:** Default click target is hardcoded 'active-tab' which can replace the current terminal unexpectedly. 'Open in current tab' uses modeOverride:'split-pane' — wording vs behavior (split) may confuse. PresetsBar is gated behind a setting that defaults off (getShowPresetsBar can be undefined/false), so the bar is hidden until explicitly enabled. Mixed RU/EN labels in the manage menu ('Manage Presets' tooltip + 'Show Preset Bar' EN, but 'Управление пресетами' RU).

### Branch/Project color menu (PROJECT color, sets thumbnail tint — NOT a chat background tint)
- **Entry:** WorkspaceSidebar (v1) -> ProjectSection -> ProjectHeader context menu -> 'Set Color' submenu -> ColorSelector(variant="menu").
- **Состояние:** ColorSelector renders the 12 PROJECT_COLORS (Red..Slate, hex values) plus a 'default' gray sentinel. 'menu' variant = ContextMenuItem rows with a swatch + name + check; 'inline' variant = round swatch buttons with hover:scale-110 + selected ring. In ProjectHeader, the submenu calls handleColorChange -> useUpdateProject patch {color}. The color drives ProjectThumbnail (the small project icon/avatar in the sidebar), NOT any chat/pane background.
- **Gaps:** There is NO 'chat background tint by branch color' in the codebase. The requested 'chat background tint' does not exist as a feature: panes/chat use flat `bg-background`; the only background richness comes from the global WallpaperBackground + .glass translucency, which is workspace/branch-agnostic. Project color is purely the thumbnail accent. If a per-branch chat tint is the intent, it is unbuilt. ColorSelector also has no custom-hex input — fixed 12-swatch palette only.

### Glass background / vibrancy + wallpaper (the actual 'chat background')
