- **Entry:** WallpaperBackground mounted once in _authenticated/layout.tsx; .glass class toggled on document root from Appearance settings; tokens defined in globals.css.
- **Состояние:** globals.css defines --surface-opacity (default 1) and --backdrop-blur (default 0) so the app is opaque until glass is enabled. `:root.glass` sets opacity 0.3, blur 24px, saturate 1.8; `.glass`/`.glass-panel` use color-mix(background/card, transparent) + backdrop-filter blur+saturate, plus a liquid-glass specular box-shadow (inset top hairline + inner outline + drop shadow). Crucially there are UNLAYERED `:root.glass .bg-background/.bg-sidebar/.bg-card` overrides (with :not guards for dialog/sheet/drawer content and authored /alpha utilities) that make every opaque surface translucent so the wallpaper shows through — the comment says this fixes a prior 'black panel over wallpaper' bug. WallpaperBackground boots the wallpaper store (hydrate + rotation timer) and renders the fixed, negative-z WallpaperLayer; renders nothing when no wallpaper selected.
- **Gaps:** Glass relies on the BrowserWindow being created with native vibrancy + transparency in main process; if the window isn't transparent, `.glass body{background:transparent}` yields a black backdrop (the exact bug the unlayered rules guard against). Dialog/alert/sheet/drawer are intentionally excluded from translucency for legibility — if a popover/menu uses bg-background instead of --popover it would wrongly turn translucent. Wallpaper is global, not per-workspace. Whether glass is currently enabled by default is a runtime setting, not in CSS.

### Branch-name vs project-name typography
- **Entry:** v1 sidebar: ProjectHeader (project name) + WorkspaceListItem (branch/workspace name) + WorkspaceRow (list view).
- **Состояние:** Project name: ProjectHeader row is `text-sm font-medium` (12px*... actually Tailwind text-sm=0.875rem) with the name in a plain truncate span and a muted tabular-nums workspace count. Branch/workspace name in the tree: WorkspaceListItem uses `text-[13px] leading-tight`, active = `text-foreground font-medium`, inactive = muted; branch sub-line uses `text-[11px] font-mono text-muted-foreground/60`. WorkspaceRow (list view) uses `text-sm truncate text-foreground/80` for the name and `text-[10px] font-mono` for +/- diff stats. The global UI font is 'SF UI Display Pro' (sans) at 12px base; mono stack is Geist Mono/Monospace Argon/Victor Mono.
- **Gaps:** Size scale is slightly inconsistent: project name text-sm (14px) vs branch text-[13px] vs WorkspaceRow name text-sm — three different sizes for conceptually peer labels. font-medium is applied to project always but to branch only when active, so hierarchy reads inconsistently. Branch path sub-line is mono while names are sans — intentional but worth confirming against the Victor Mono intent. No shared typography token; sizes are ad-hoc per component.

### Thinking / reasoning-effort control
- **Entry:** Chat composer footer: ChatComposerControls (both V1 components/Chat and V2 WorkspaceChatInterface copies) renders ReasoningLevelSlider.
- **Состояние:** The live control is ReasoningLevelSlider (@rox/ui/motion): a pill with a BrainIcon + 'Размышление' caption and an inline segmented radiogroup of 5 levels — Выкл / Низкий / Средний / Высокий / Макс — backed by ThinkingLevel = off|low|medium|high|xhigh. Active segment tracked by a framer-motion shared-layout marker (layoutId 'reasoning-marker', motionSpring.snappy, respects reduced-motion via useShouldAnimate('essential')). Caption dims to muted when level is 'off'. It is placed in PromptInputTools next to PermissionModePicker and ModelPicker, styled with PILL_BUTTON_CLASS.
- **Gaps:** Two parallel thinking controls exist in @rox/ui: ReasoningLevelSlider (segmented, RU labels) which is the one used, and ThinkingToggle (dropdown, EN labels Off/Low/Medium/High/Max) which is NOT used by the composer — dead/duplicate component, divergent labels & language. The control is duplicated across V1 and V2 ChatComposerControls copies, so any change must be made twice. Label localization split: slider is RU, the unused toggle is EN.

### File-tree panel (Files tab) + background
- **Entry:** v1: WorkspaceLayout -> RightSidebar (ResizablePanel) -> FilesView. v2: v2-workspace WorkspaceSidebar FilesTab.
- **Состояние:** RightSidebar is `<aside class='h-full flex flex-col overflow-hidden'>` with a 10px header bar (`bg-background border-b`, tabs Изменения/Файлы + expand + close). FilesView uses @headless-tree (asyncDataLoader+selection+expandAll) over trpc filesystem.listDirectory, with FileTreeToolbar (search/new file/new folder/collapse/refresh), live file-watch refresh (useWorkspaceFileEvents, 75ms debounce), rename/new/delete inline inputs, and a context menu. Rows are FileTreeItem at ROW_HEIGHT/TREE_INDENT. Empty state: 'No workspace selected'.
- **Gaps:** The file-tree panel body has NO explicit background — only the 10px header is `bg-background`; the `<aside>` and the tree scroll container (`outline-none`, `h-full overflow-auto`) are transparent, so the panel paints over whatever is behind it (the layout `bg-background`, or under .glass the wallpaper). This is the likely 'file-tree panel background' issue: in glass mode the tree has no panel surface of its own and can look unbounded/see-through. Mixed RU/EN strings ('No workspace selected', 'New File/Folder' EN vs tab labels RU). V1 FilesView and v2 FilesTab are separate implementations.

### Pipeline editor (graph canvas + node config + validation)
- **Entry:** /_authenticated/_dashboard/pipelines/$pipelineId -> PipelineEditor.
- **Состояние:** FULLY FUNCTIONAL, not stubbed. Editor shell = toolbar (back, name+slug, validity Badge, SaveIndicator, roles-panel toggle) + xyflow Canvas + right aside (NodeInspector when a node is selected, else Tabs Роли/Триггеры/Запуски). NODES ARE ADDED two ways: (1) PipelineCanvas top-left Panel buttons 'Агент/Цикл/Подтверждение/Финал' -> onAddNode(kind); (2) RoleLibraryPanel onAddRole -> addNode('agent_run', roleSlug, label). addNode() in PipelineEditor mints a `${kind}_${rand}` block id, positions it in a cascade by block count, writes into RoxWorkflowState.blocks, applies the change, and auto-selects it to open the inspector. Edits round-trip through graph-adapter (stateToNodes/flowToState) and are debounce-saved (800ms) via trpc.pipeline.updateGraph. VALIDATION/PROBLEMS come from the SERVER: trpc.pipeline.validate query returns {valid, issues:WorkflowIssue[]} (from @rox/workflow-core); updateGraph success invalidates the validate query. Toolbar shows 'граф валиден' or 'N проблем(ы)'; NodeInspector filters issues by blockId and lists them per node. NODE CONFIG IS ENABLED and editable: AgentNodeForm has a role Select (agentRole.list, '__none__' sentinel, 'роль не найдена' hint), model-override Input, max-turns (1-200 clamp) and temperature (0-2 clamp) Inputs, all writing subBlocks via patch.patchNode. The only disabled control is the per-node 'Узел включён' Switch which is correctly hidden for the immutable 'start' node, and the delete button hidden for start.
- **Gaps:** Node config is NOT generally disabled — if any field appeared disabled it would be: (a) inputs only commit on blur/Enter (no live save, can feel unresponsive); (b) the role Select shows nothing useful if agentRole.list is empty/unauthorized (no roles -> only 'Без роли'), making the agent node look unconfigurable; (c) AgentNodeForm uses useCloudTrpc (cloud API) so without an authenticated v2 cloud session the role list, validate, and updateGraph all fail silently-ish (toast on save error only). Validation is server-authoritative, so offline/blocked cloud = no validity badge and stale issues. blockType coercion: unknown persisted types fall back to 'agent_run' rendering. Pipelines live entirely in the V2/cloud surface.

### Notes editor (Suite)
- **Entry:** Suite NotesView (three-pane: notebooks / notes / reader-editor).
- **Состояние:** NotesView is a grid `[200px 240px 1fr]`: notebooks column, notes column (with FTS search via notes.searchNotes, create-note dialog), and a reader pane. The reader pane is EDITABLE and STAYS EDITABLE after create: the editor component is CollaborativeNoteEditor, mounted keyed by note id, with the body in editorMarkdown state and autosave (800ms debounce -> notes.updateNote, flush-on-unmount). After createNote succeeds, setActiveNoteId(row.id) selects the new note and the reader immediately shows the editable editor — no read-only lock. CollaborativeNoteEditor wraps an ExperimentalFeatureGate('collaboration.editor'): gate CLOSED (default) -> PlainNoteTextarea (controlled, `min-h-[55vh] resize-none font-mono`); gate OPEN + active org -> YjsNoteTextarea bound to a Liveblocks room (noteRoomId) via @rox/collab createNoteYjsBinding for real-time co-editing, falling back to PlainNoteTextarea when no org.
- **Gaps:** The create-note dialog has its OWN separate markdown Textarea (noteMarkdown) distinct from the live editor — two editing entry points for the same field. The editor is a raw monospace Textarea (no rich/markdown WYSIWYG, no toolbar) even though body is markdown; SnippetText only renders highlighted search snippets, not a formatted note. Collaborative path is gated off by default, so multiplayer is invisible unless the experiment flag is on. Mixed RU UI strings throughout. Notes are a V2/cloud (useCloudTrpc) surface — needs cloud auth.

### Mail / Email view + width constraint
- **Entry:** Suite EmailView (standalone /email route, or embedded in InboxView).
- **Состояние:** EmailView wraps content in SuiteScreen with className="max-w-6xl" — this is the width constraint. SuiteScreen base is `mx-auto w-full max-w-5xl px-6 py-6`, and the `cn(...,className)` merge means EmailView's max-w-6xl WINS (later class), so mail content centers at max-w-6xl (~1152px). Inside: a two-column grid `[280px 1fr]` (thread list + reader). Bodies are fetched from R2 via useMailBody; HTML is DOMPurify-sanitized (sanitizeMailHtml) and injected into an isolated clipped container `max-h-[60vh] overflow-auto [&_a]:underline [&_img]:max-w-full`; text renders escaped. Compose dialog (to/subject/body) via mail.send. Attachments via presigned mail.getAttachmentUrl.
- **Gaps:** Width override depends on Tailwind class-order precedence (max-w-6xl listed after max-w-5xl in cn) rather than an explicit prop — fragile if the merge utility or class order changes, both max-w-5xl and max-w-6xl are emitted. Sanitized HTML uses dangerouslySetInnerHTML (justified by DOMPurify) — correct but security-sensitive. The reader is a 280px+1fr split inside a max-w-6xl shell, so on wide windows the message column can get very wide while the thread list stays fixed. V2/cloud surface (useCloudTrpc); RU strings.

### App icon assets
- **Entry:** src/resources/build/icons (packaged app icons) + src/renderer/assets/app-icons (editor/IDE logos for OpenIn).
- **Состояние:** build/icons holds icon.png (1024x1024 RGB), 128/256/512/1024 PNGs, icon.icns (mac), icon.ico (win), plus -dev and -canary variants of icns/ico/png. The app icon art is a black rounded-square with a white high-contrast stylized woman's face (Transistor/Supergiant-style key art). renderer/assets/app-icons contains 3rd-party editor logos (vscode, cursor, zed, jetbrains family, ghostty, warp, iterm, finder...) used by OpenInButton/OpenInExternalDropdown, plus a preset-icons subdir for agent preset glyphs (getPresetIcon, light/dark).
- **Gaps:** icon.png, icon-dev.png, icon-canary.png are BYTE-IDENTICAL (md5 53b282a8..., 72185 bytes) and icon.icns/icon-dev.icns/icon-canary.icns are also byte-identical (md5 29de6c39...). So the dev and canary build channels are NOT visually differentiated from production — you cannot tell a dev/canary dock icon apart from the release build. icon.ico is also nearly identical across channels (icon.ico 370070b vs dev/canary .ico 410598b, only the .ico differs slightly). If channel-distinct icons are intended (common for Electron dev builds), they are unimplemented.
